From: Tedx CHARUSAT <tedx@charusat.ac.in>
Content:
Dear CHARUSAT Family Members,
Greetings!!

Faculty of Technology and Engineering (FTE), Charotar University of Science
and Technology (CHARUSAT) is going to host *TEDx CHARUSAT *on September 24,
2024. This event promises to be inspiring and thought-provoking, showcasing
innovative ideas and compelling stories from a diverse range of speakers.

*Event Details:*

   - *Date:* September 24, 2024
   - *Venue:* CHARUSAT Campus (Exact venue details will be shared on later
   date)
   - *Time:* 10:00 AM - 4:00 PM

*TEDx CHARUSAT* aims to bring together the brightest minds, fostering an
environment where ideas can be shared, discussed, and celebrated. Under the
theme *"Ingenious Creations",* we will explore groundbreaking ideas and
revolutionary innovations that have the potential to change the world. We
believe that every participant will leave the event with new perspectives
and a renewed sense of curiosity.

*Call for Speaker Recommendations:* As we prepare for this exciting event,
we are looking for identification of exceptional speakers. If any staff
member has any close contacts or knows of individuals who have a powerful
story, innovative idea, or unique perspective to share, please refer them
to us. We are looking for speakers who can inspire, challenge, and engage
our audience.

*How to Recommend a Speaker:* Please send your speaker recommendations
to  *tedx@charusat.ac.in *by July 25, 2024. Kindly include the following
details:

   - Name of the speaker
   - Contact information (email and phone number)
   - A brief description of their background and the topic they would speak
   on.
   - A video link to the TEDx /Any other prominent talk given by the speaker

Your input is invaluable, and we are confident that TEDx CHARUSAT will be
an unforgettable event.

Thank you for your support and participation. We look forward to seeing you
at TEDx CHARUSAT!

*For any query/concerns/information *kindly get in touch with *Dr. Nikita
Bhatt* (nikitabhatt.ce@charusat.ac.in) |* Dr. Dweepna Garg* (
dweepnagarg.ce@charusat.ac.in) | *Dr. Kirti Makwana *(
kirtimakwana.mba@charusat.ac.in) | *Ms. Pinal Patel* (
pinalpatel.cv@charusat.ac.in).

Best Regards,

Dr. Vijay Chaudhary, Dr. Bankim Patel & Dr. Trushit Upadhyaya
-- 
I/c Principal
Chandubhai S Patel Institute of Technology
Faculty of Technology & Engineering
Charotar University of Science & Technology (CHARUSAT)
CHARUSAT Campus, Changa, 388421
Petlad, Anand
Gujarat, India.

Download and Install

Download instructions are available here:
http://www.mathworks.com/matlabcentral/answers/98268

The installation will begin as soon as the download is complete.

Activate your Software

Once the software is installed MATLAB will attempt to activate itself. You
will be required to enter your MathWorks account credentials again for
activation. If the software does not automatically attempt to activate, you
will need to launch the activation client:
http://www.mathworks.com/matlabcentral/answers/99457-how-do-i-activate-matl=
ab

In some setups, such as one where a firewall is in place or a proxy is
filtering all network activity, you may need to activate MATLAB manually.
Instructions for manual activation can be found here:
http://www.mathworks.com/matlabcentral/answers/105854

Resonant frequency decreases

*

Current/voltage drops to ln(e) times the initial value (ln: natural Log)


Current/voltage drops to e times the initial value


Current/voltage drops to e^2 times the initial value

Consider the following situations:
(1) two capacitors connected in parallel with each other and then in series  
with a resistor having resistance R.
(2) Two capacitors are connected in series with each other and then in

*

If the diameter of a coil is increased, what happens to the density of the  
magnetic field lines inside the coil? *


Increases


Decreases


Remains the same


Disappears

what happens to the magnetic field strength at its center?

*


It doubles


It halves


It quadruples


It remains the same

total magnetic field?

*


Coil with a larger diameter


Coil with a smaller diameter

Both coils will experience the same magnetic field strength


Biot-Savart's Law is used to determine the:

*


The electric field around a charged particle


Magnetic field around a current-carrying conductor


The force between two charged particles


The potential difference across a resistor


According to Biot-Savart's Law, the magnetic field (B) produced by a  
current element (dl) is:


Directly proportional to the current (I) and inversely proportional to the  
distance from the current element (r)


Inversely proportional to the current (I) and directly proportional to the  
distance from the current element (r)


Directly proportional to the current (I) and the distance from the current  
element (r)


Inversely proportional to the current (I) and the distance from the current  
element (r)

From: Sports CHARUSAT <sports.officer@charusat.ac.in>
Content:
Dear All,

Greeting of CHARUSAT Sports


Report on Pankti Akbari Achievement in Khel Mahakumbh-2024 State level
Taekwondo Tournament. We are thrilled to announce that Pankti
Akbari(23CS001) a student of the Computer Science Engineering department at
the Chandubhai S. Patel Institute of Technology, affiliated with Charotar
University of Science and Technology (CHARUSAT), has demonstrated
outstanding prowess in Taekwondo.

Pankti secured the 1st place at the district level Khel Mahakumbh Taekwondo
Tournament held in Surat. Building on this remarkable performance, she went
on to achieve a Gold Medal at the State Level tournament on 16 May, 2024

Her dedication, hard work, and exceptional skill have not only brought her
personal accolades but have also made our university proud. We extend our
heartiest congratulations to Pankti Akbari for this significant achievement
and wish her continued success in all her future endeavours.


Congratulations, Pankti!

CHARUSAT - Proud to Nurture Champions



--
Dr.Pritesh Patel
Assistant Director of Physical Education and Sports
CHARUSAT Physical Education and Sports Section
(A constituent of CHARUSAT)
*Accredited with "Grade A+" by NAAC, GOI*
*Accredited with Centre of Excellence by GOG*

From: Naina Parmar <nainaparmar.dcs@charusat.ac.in>
Content:
Students learn to build hands-on AI projects. Earn a certificate and an
internship upon completion.

Dear all



I want to express my gratitude for the support you provided in reaching out
to students during the past few months. Professors like you have gone above
and beyond to support students not only with their coursework but also
helping them learn the latest technology beyond what is taught in regular
course curriculum. We appreciate you for this.



Some time back we launched Artificial Intelligence (AI) training and have
been thrilled with the response. In just a short amount of time, hundreds
of students have enrolled. Especially with the launch of ChatGPT, AI is
becoming increasingly pervasive across all industries, from healthcare and
finance to entertainment and transportation.



Our AI training and internship program offers students the necessary skills
to secure high-paying jobs in this field. Considering this, we are
launching a scholarship and internship program for our AI training and
internship. Please share this opportunity with your students.


What is the Artificial Intelligence (AI) scholarship and internship program=
?

   - As part of this program, the qualifying students of Devang Patel
   Institute of Advance Technology and Research can *join the Artificial
   Intelligence (AI) online video training at an 80% discount.* While the
   regular fee of the training is Rs.8,600/-, the qualifying students can g=
et
   it at just Rs.1,750/-.

   - Students have to visit https://info.boltiot.com/aischolarship to answer the scholarship test.


What are some of the activities that students will perform as part of this
AI training?

   - Learn concepts of Artificial Intelligence (AI) from the basics. No
   previous knowledge is required.
   - Learn programming languages like Python, HTML and Javascript.
   - During the training, we will be available to solve any doubts or
   queries.
   - Students will build 6 different hands-on projects, such as Their own
   ChatGPT, AI Recipe generator, AI Software coding helper, AI Image Genera=
tor
   and many more...
   - They will also build innovative Artificial Intelligence (AI) projects
   by applying the learnings of the training in their field.


Why should the students avail this scholarship?

   - This four weeks of online video training is *excellent for those who
   want to start with Artificial Intelligence (AI)* because it teaches them
   to build projects from the basics.

   - *Certificate:* upon completion of the training, which can be submitted
   as part of university rules as well as during the job application proces=
s.

   - *Work on industrial projects: *The students will work on the most
   popular AI Platform by Open AI. The same platform is the base for ChatGP=
T
   and is used by thousands of MNCs across the globe.

   - *Guaranteed internship upon training **completion: *This internship
   certificate can be submitted to the college if the university rules requ=
ire
   them to do so.


Other critical points:

   - *The option of full refund:* In case the students are not happy with
   the training offered to them, then they can get a full refund as per the
   refund policy. This ensures that there is no risk for students or the
   faculty involved in the process.

   - *Lifetime access:* Students can register now and start the training
   after the exams or at any other time. They can also take a break in betw=
een.

   - Link to answer the scholarship quiz:
   https://info.boltiot.com/aischolarship The last date to avail the scholarship is Tuesday, 20th of February 2024.



My team and I are excited to teach Devang Patel Institute of Advance
Technology and Research students about Artificial Intelligence (AI). If you
have any questions, please reply to this email or call us at
(+91)8881197198 and press 4 to speak with us. I'm happy to provide any
further information you need.



Regards,
Rohit TS
Software Developer - Bolt IoT

Bolt IoT (Inventrom Private Limited), 79, 11th Cross Rd, Binnamangala,
Indiranagar, Bengaluru, Karnataka 560038, India, (+91)8881197198

*Dear Students of * *CHARUSAT*
*(ALL  DEPARTMENTS 1st to 4th year**)*
*[ MANDATORY INTERNSHIP ]*

Greetings!

We are pleased to share with you that our company, TEACHNOOK, is
collaborating with Cognizance (IIT Roorkee) to offer a unique 2-month
Training + Internship  Program. This advanced program will provide you with
the missing practical skills that you need to enhance your career.

 We are enrolling only *LIMITED STUDENTS *in the program for *CHARUSAT**.*

*To know more information join in whatsapp group:*

*https://chat.whatsapp.com/GoB39BYWJ5A7fpBJlti0NG *


*It is Mandatory for students to fill out the form, if you get shortlisted
you will be getting a call from our HR Team:*
https://forms.gle/wXeFXk2pcBC9rXx86


*FIND THE BELOW ATTACHMENTS FOR REFERENCE:*
*First month*: IIT training has been designed in the form of Live lectures
along with living mentorship from industry professionals. (Login
credentials will be provided to students after registration)
*No Prerequisites Required.*


*Second month*: Internship with live mentorship for projects from
professionals. The LIVE INDUSTRY PROJECT will be giving students experience
in solving real-world problems.

Project 1:- 10 individual projects assigned to each intern which they have
to complete with their mentor .

Project 2:-  Capstone Project: It's a group project assigned to a
group of 15 interns. For each intern particular work will be assigned to
them they have to work on it.
(Essential data and materials required for the project will be provided by
the company side itself)

Here are two types of Classes we are providing:

1. Blended Program/Recorded classes: You will receive recorded sessions,
whatever doubts you have you can clear it in live doubt clearing sessions
which will be organized every weekend.

2. Mentor led/Live classes: You will be having live zoom classes at 6:30PM
 for 2 to 3 days a week. You will get your recorded sessions as well
LMS(Learning Management System) portal where you will have access to it for
6 months.

After Completion of the program the student shall receive a:

=E2=9C=85 Program completion certificate issued by  Cognizance (IIT Roorkee=
) and
Verified By Wipro DICE ID.
=E2=9C=85 Co-Branded Internship certificate from Top MNCs.
=E2=9C=85 100% Placement Assistance.
=E2=9C=85 Access to a growing community.

*Congratulations! To Already registered** students*, You've taken the first
step towards a brighter future. Don't miss out on this chance to take your
career to the next level. Spread the word to your friends and classmates so
they can benefit too!

Dear Contributors,
We're back with another exciting surprise for you! =F0=9F=8E=81
We=E2=80=99re thrilled to announce the launch of our latest feature: Custom=
ized Badges! =F0=9F=8F=85=F0=9F=8E=89
With this new update, contributors working on open-source projects can now =
create and personalise badges to highlight their achievements, contribution=
s, and milestones. This feature lets you showcase your hard work and get no=
ticed by potential connections on OPN.
Key Features:
=E2=9C=A8Shareable: Easily share your badges on social media and other plat=
forms.
=E2=9C=A8Customizable: Make your badges truly yours with personalised desig=
ns.
How to Get Started?
Navigate to the Leaderboard: Leaderboard Link [ https://substack.com/redire=
ct/f3e2c2ec-8f6b-4c2e-8e24-1163952d019b?j=3DeyJ1IjoiM3Yxd3RxIn0.pS6nfe3axVn=
bdKqBjOVXmoGAY01Y5n5tFxjxFZEfFWU ]
Hover over your score to view your badges. =F0=9F=8F=85
Click on a badge to download and share it as an image.
Share your badge on LinkedIn, Twitter, or your GitHub Readme profile!

 will receive free XYZ domain coupons plus a free subscription to the Wiref=
rame app.

Google Calendar now shows events from Gmail



Google Calendar can show events such as reservations and flights, that  
Gmail creates from messages you receive. Your calendar now shows this event  
from Gmail:

ML Connect: AWS on Tue Jul 23, 2024 at 10:00am

Only you can see an event from Gmail unless you change the event's  
visibility. You can also change the default visibility of events from Gmail  
in Calendar settings.

To stop seeing these events in Calendar or change their default visibility,  
go to Events from Gmail in Calendar settings. To stop Gmail from creating  
these events, you must also turn off Smart features and personalization in  
Gmail settings. Learn more at  
https://support.google.com/calendar/?p=events_from_gmail about events from  
Gmail and how to control them.

This is the only notification youâll get about events from Gmail. In  
the future, Calendar wonât send you an email when Gmail creates a new  
event. = = = Google Calendar no=

From: Pradipsinh Zala <pradipzala.cs@charusat.ac.in>
Content:
Dear Students,



Greetings!



You must be aware that the Faculty of Humanities offers a *2 Credit *
Compulsory *Course on Liberal Arts.*


Please be informed that the liberal arts course opted by you will be
taught in the *Workshop Mode *(9:10 am to 4:30 pm) during* 05, 06, and 07
March, 2023 *at CHARUSAT Campus, Changa.



*Please note that if you fail to attend the workshop, complete the tasks,
activities and assignments, you may FAIL in the course and get a BACKLOG.*



*Please make a note of following:*


   - Ensure that your Liberal Arts Course Registration is completed on the
   E-Governance and you have elected / registered for one of the Liberal Ar=
ts
   Courses i.e. Painting, Photography, Media and Graphic Design, Contempora=
ry
   Dance, and Dramatics.
   - Each course of Liberal Arts is a 2 Credit Course.
   - *You are required to collect a Kit*. The kit distribution is scheduled
   on *March 04, 2024* (from 9:30 am to 4:00 pm) in different slots. The
   venue for the kit distribution will be Indukaka Ipcowala Institute of
   Management. You will be informed about your slot for kit collection by y=
our
   institute faculty coordinator.
   -  Students must bring the Kit every day and take care of the materials
   and instruments given to them. In case, if something is lost, you will b=
e
   required to manage it.
   - *Ensure to maintain 100% attendance and completion of the assigned
   tasks/assignments / submissions during the liberal arts workshop. Failin=
g
   to do so may result in FF Grade/backlog in this course. *
   - Students need to report on time (at least 10 minutes before the
   stipulated time).
   - They must perform the practical or do the tasks assigned to them.
   -  As the external Resource Persons are invited, you are also required
   to maintain discipline and decorum befitting the students of a universit=
y
   and professional programs.
   - It is required that every student carry their own Identity Card and
   wears it during all three days of the workshop.
   - Details of the syllabus for the opted course, the evaluation scheme,
   and other instructions will be provided to the students in their kit as
   well as via email.
   - Ensure that you have access to your Teams / Google Classroom account
   as that will be required for further communications and submissions.
   - Follow the instructions / guidance given by the Resource Persons /
   Faculty Coordinators.

Feel free to contact Dr. Pradipsinh B Zala, Mobile Number: 9510963189
(Institute Coordinator) in case of any queries.



Happy Learning! =F0=9F=98=80=F0=9F=98=80



With regards,



*Dr. Pradipsinh B Zala*

Assistant Professor

Faculty of Humanities

*Charotar University of Science & Technology (CHARUSAT) *

Changa-388421 | Ta. Petlad,

Dist. Anand | Gujarat

*Mobile No: +91-95109 63189*

Content:
Stories from your activity

Question: Is a 80cc 2-stroke engine faster than a 50cc 4-stroke engine?


Answer from Jan Kannemacher

Dear Students,

It brings me immense joy to extend my heartfelt congratulations to each one
of you on your remarkable performance in the recent *Sem-2 B.Tech CSE
University exams.*

Please find attached a* list of toppers *in the recent examination.

As you move forward in your academic pursuits, remember that *learning is a
continuous journey*, and your thirst for knowledge will undoubtedly lead

will make in the field of Computer Science and Engineering.

*Best wishes!!!*
*Notes: *

   examinations were considered.

that you need to enhance your career.

We are enrolling only *LIMITED STUDENTS *in the program.

you will be getting a call from our HR Team:*

LINK:- https://forms.gle/NF1cgFGe5ohF5LtV9

*First month : *IIT training has been designed in the form of Live lectures
along with living mentorship from industry professionals. (Login
credentials will be provided to students after registration)
No Prerequisites Required.

*Second month : Internship with live mentorship for projects from
professionals. The LIVE INDUSTRY PROJECT will be giving students experience
in solving real-world problems.*

*Project 1:- 10 individual projects assigned to each intern which they have
to complete with their mentor .*

*Project 2:-  Capstone Project: It's a group project assigned to a
group of 15 interns. For each intern particular work will be assigned to
them they have to work on it.*
(Essential data and materials required for the project will be provided by
the company side itself)

*Here are two types of Classes we are providing:*

*1. Blended Program/Recorded classes: You will receive recorded sessions,
whatever doubts you have you can clear it in live doubt clearing sessions
which will be organized every weekend.*

*2. Mentor led/Live classes: You will be having live zoom classes at 6:30PM
 for 2 to 3 days a week. You will get your recorded sessions as well*
LMS(Learning Management System) portal where you will have access to it for
6 months.

   - Batch Start Date: 7th of Every Month.

From: Cyber Kavach <cyberkavach.cse@charusat.ac.in>
Content:
Hello Hackers!

Here are the solutions for all the challenges as promised :)
I have zipped and attached all the necessary files for you to reproduce the
challenges locally.
These are all the intended solutions. There are other unintended ways as
well that we hadn't taken into consideration. Well done if you managed to
solve a challenge with a new way that is not mentioned here.
Reach out to Het Soni (21cs068@charusat.edu.in, +91 95109 56552) for any
queries regarding the CTF.


** Welcome*
Solution: You had to visit the /robots.txt file on the same domain where
the CTF was hosted.


* *I can't SEEEEE IT*
Solution: From the source code of the page you can see it is fetching the
flag from a remote API.
Check the Network activity with inspect when you click the get flag button.


* *Secure Login*
Solution: You can edit frontend html from inspect. Remove 'disabled' from
all html form elements to enter text into the fields. Entering default
credentials 'admin:password' and pressing the login button fetched the flag
but didn't display on the front end. You again had to see the network
activity and check the response from the remote API.


* *Encoding is not encryption!*
Challenge: VEhNe0NyeXB0MEJAYnl9
Solution: Base64 encoded string.


* *Stupid Chemistry*
Challenge: 39 EA 1 6 2 M 53 16 TR 39
Solution: Periodic Table cipher - dcode.fr/atomic-number-substitution


** QR Busted!*
Solution: QR codes are in a pattern. Fill in the missing two corners by
copying the top right corner and scan it for the solution.


** Find me if you can*
Challenge: "Co-lead of The Hackers Meetup, Harshiv Kinariwala doesn't
follow security policies and posts company secrets on social media!
Can you believe that!
Find that secret to get the flag."
Solution: twitter.com/h_kinariwala


* *The Third Eye*
Solution: A mp3 file is given. Use tools like audacity or skel to visualize
it. It was Spectrogram Stegnography.
Many have submitted the flag correctly but you were supposed to replace
whitespaces with an underscore ( _ ).


** RUN ME*
Solution: The problem category was pwn where you are given an executable
and you have to understand it's nature and logic and exploit it.
Here in the given linux executable, you have to brute force the inputs by
creating a local bash script that would input numbers one by one and output
the correct number that is being accepted. Check the attached script to
understand the logic.


Thank you everyone who participated. Happy Hacking.

--

From: "Dr. Kirti Makwana" <kirtimakwana.mba@charusat.ac.in>
Content:
Dear Students,

*Greetings from CHARUSAT_FTE_DEPSTAR !!!*

We are excited to announce a workshop on *"Web Automation Testing Using
Selenium WebDriver"* by *Dr. Jaishree Tailor, Associate Manager at L&T
Technology Services, Vadodara.* This workshop will provide valuable
insights and hands-on experience in web automation testing, a crucial skill
in today's software development landscape.

*Workshop Details:*

   - *Date:* July 20, 2024, Saturday
   - *Time:* 10:00 AM onwards
   - *Venue:* Will be communicated to the registered students

*Objective:* The workshop aims to leverage awareness of industrial test
automation, covering roles, methodologies, tools, and frameworks for web
applications. It will focus on web automation techniques to streamline
testing static web forms, including element interaction, script
modularization, and unit test conversion using PyTest with Selenium and
Python.

*Learning Outcomes:* By the end of this workshop, participants will be able
to:

   - Explain the role of software testing in application development and
   differentiate between manual and test automation approaches.
   - Utilize Selenium WebDriver to automate web application testing,
   including element identification, interaction, and assertion.
   - Develop basic test automation scripts for interacting with various web
   elements (forms, dropdowns, links, etc.).
   - Apply best practices for structuring and modularizing automation
   scripts for maintainability and reusability.
   - Convert basic automation scripts into unit test scripts using the
   PyTest framework.

*Pre-requisites:* Participants are encouraged to brush up on Python syntax,
function/method design in Python, and HTML form tags, attributes, and
elements before the workshop. Please make sure you have Python 3.9 or above
and PyCharm Community Edition installed.

*Software Requirements:*

   - Python 3.9 or above: Download Here - PyCharm Community Edition: Download Here *Registration:* Please register for the workshop by *clicking here. Early registration is encouraged as
seats are limited.*

Don't miss this opportunity to enhance your skills and learn from an
industry expert. We look forward to your active participation.

Best regards,
[image: Workshop on Web Automation.png]

--

*Dr. Kirti Makwana*

Mobile:+91-9586861680

Dear Students,

Thank you for registering for the seminar on "Project Selection: For the
Upliftment of Your Career" on July 6th, 2024. In this seminar, we will
discuss how to choose projects that align with your career goals, whether
they are placements, further studies, or entrepreneurship. We will explore
futuristic technologies and provide probable definitions for various
projects.

*Dear Students,*

*Congratulations on being shortlisted for our prestigious Internship
Program!*



*We are excited to announce the launch of our 2-Month Training + Internship
program, organized by Teachnook's in collaboration with IIT Roorkee
Cognizance and designed by IBM.Here's a detailed overview of the program:*

*First Month: Training:*
-

*Engage in IBM training through live lectures and benefit from mentorship
by industry professionals.- Gain access to the IBM Portal for interactions
with trainers and peers.- Receive login credentials upon registration to
begin your learning journey.*

*Second Month: Internship:*
-
* Participate in an internship with live mentorship, working on real-world
projects under professional guidance.- This practical experience will
enhance your understanding of industry practices and hone your skills.*

* Projects:*
-

*Minor Project: An individual project to demonstrate your skills and
creativity. Dedicated sessions will help you build and enhance your
resume.- Major Project: Collaborate with a team of 15 interns on a group
project. You will be assigned specific responsibilities, and the company
will provide the necessary data and materials.*
*Third Month: Evaluation and Opportunities:*
-

*Based on your performance, you will undergo a technical interview within
the same company.- A successful interview could lead to a stipend-based
internship opportunity.*
*Program Completion Benefits:*
-









*Comprehensive training from Basic to Advanced Concepts.- Guaranteed
Internship opportunity.- 3+ Accredited Certificates with Wipro
verification.- Placement Assistance.- Completion of at least 3
Industry-based projects.- Letter of Recommendation from Project Heads.-
Mock Interviews and Group Discussions for Placement Preparation.- Access to
live and recorded sessions.- 24/7 Exclusive support.- Doubt/Query support
through live sessions.*

From: sanskruti patel <sanskrutipatel.mca@charusat.ac.in>
Content:
Dear Participants,

We are your course instructors: Dr. Sanskruti Patel and Dr. Sagar Kavaiya.

We warmly welcome you to our certification course on "Machine Learning and
Data Science: From Beginner to Expert," which will commence on June 29,
2024, with the first session scheduled at 9:15 AM.

Please join the session using the following link :
https://meet.google.com/wxt-mgjz-tjk

Please note that we will be using the same link for all sessions throughout
the course.

To facilitate our learning and collaboration, we have created a Google
Classroom. Please join the classroom using the following link:
https://classroom.google.com/c/Njk3MDUzNDA1NTAw?cjc=c7fh33a

The course will be offered in a blended mode, combining theory sessions
with hands-on implementation. We will be using Google Colab for the
implementation exercises. Additionally, the Google Classroom will serve as
a hub for sharing course resources, including notes, code, references, and
more.

You will find the detailed schedule attached to this message, and it is
also available in the Google Classroom.

Looking forward to an engaging and fruitful learning journey with all of
you!

Best regards,
Dr. Sanskruti Patel and Dr. Sagar Kavaiya
--
Dr. Sanskruti Patel
Associate Professor
Smt. Chandaben Mohanbhai Patel Institute of Computer Applications
Faculty of Computer Science and Applications
Charotar University of Science and Technology
Changa.

--

Dear Students,

As you have registered for the upcoming session, I request each of you to
register on the NDLI Member Portal for your e-certificate. Failure to
register will result in not receiving the participation certificate.

For registration, existing NDLI Club members of your institute can follow
these steps:

1. Click on Member Login Member login link .
2. Enter your registered NDLI Club e-mail ID (username) and password.
3. After logging in, click on the Events section and select the event name.
4. Check the eligibility button available on the right side of the event.
5. Once it shows that you are eligible, click on the Participate button.

You will receive the e-Certificate of Participation on your NDLI portal.
For any queries, please write to jaypatel.dce@charusat.ac.in.

Thanks,
NDLI Club of Devang Patel Institute of Advance Technology and Research
(DEPSTAR)

Teachnook is conducting an *AICTE APPROVED* Internship for STUDENTS, Kindly
go through this join the group, and fill out the form ASAP.
Register before Slots get filled.



*Greetings!*

*We are pleased to share that our company is collaborating with INSTITUTION
to offer a unique 2-month Training + Internship  Program. This advanced
program will provide you with the practical skills that you need to enhance
your career.*

 We are enrolling only *LIMITED STUDENTS* in the program.



*It is Mandatory for students to fill out the form, if you get shortlisted
you will get a call from our HR Team:GOOGLE
FORM: https://forms.gle/WsnTxKdcRwpD8ZXw6 *


*To know more information join in WhatsApp group:*

*https://chat.whatsapp.com/JKAouyKSlFdJ6SJjGoIKOm *


*FIND THE BELOW ATTACHMENTS FOR REFERENCE:*

*First month: *IIT training has been designed in the form of Live lectures
along with living mentorship from industry professionals. (Login
credentials will be provided to students after registration)
No Prerequisites Required.

*Second month: *Internship with live mentorship for projects from
professionals. The LIVE INDUSTRY PROJECT will give students experience in
solving real-world problems.

*Project 1:- *10 individual projects are assigned to each intern, which
they must complete with their mentor.

*Project 2:-  *Capstone Project: It's a group project assigned to a
group of 10-12 interns. For each intern particular work will be assigned to
them they have to work on it.
(Essential data and materials required for the project will be provided by
the company side itself)

*Here are two types of Sessions we are providing:*

*1. Blended Program/Recorded Sessions: *You will receive recorded sessions,
whatever doubts you have you can clear them in live doubt-clearing sessions
which will be organized every weekend.

*2. Mentor-led/Live Sessions: *You will be having live Zoom classes after 7
PM for 2 to 3 days a week. You will get your recorded sessions as well
*LMS(Learning Management System)* portal which you will have access to for
6 months.

After Completion of the program, the student shall receive :

Verified By Wipro DICE ID.

Dear Students,

We hope you are in good health and enthusiastic about the interview process
within the club. As you may be aware, we are in the process of selecting
new team members for various positions to steer the club to greater
heights. We are now excited to welcome you to the interview process.

The available positions are as follows:
1. Lead and Co-Lead
2. Technical Team
3. Content Team
4. Graphics and Media Team

For the positions of *Lead and Co-lead, **the selections will be conducted
offline*. For the *other positions, the selection will be conducted online.*



*Interview Dates:Lead and Co-lead: 6th February, 2024 (Wednesday)Other
Positions: 7th February, 2024 (Thursday)*

Venue and timings will be communicated soon.

For the interview, we encourage you to come prepared with basic knowledge
about the responsibilities of the position you're applying for.
Additionally, *please bring along any relevant previous work or projects
you've undertaken*, particularly for positions 2 through 4 (Technical Team,
Content Team, Graphic Team, and Social Team). This will provide us with
insight into your skills and capabilities.

Your unique talents and perspectives will contribute significantly to the
club's success, and we are eager to see what you can bring to the table.

If you have any questions or concerns regarding the interview process,
please don't hesitate to reach out to us.

Best regards,

*Program Highlights: *

Gain real-world experience in cutting-edge technologies with our Tech
Domain Internship. Work alongside industry experts on live projects,
sharpen your programming skills, and learn the latest trends in AI, ML,
IoT, and more. Collaborate with a dynamic team, solve complex problems, and
innovate solutions that make a difference. Get hands-on with
industry-standard tools and technologies, preparing you for a successful
career in the tech industry.


*To ensure your participation and make the most out of this opportunity,
please make sure to fill out the application form: *


         Application form: *https://forms.gle/RPMmwLY5KwDwLRGe *


*Program promises:*


   - *36+ hours of live training*
   - *10+ live hands-on Minor project*
   - *1 live capstone project*
   - *Live doubt-clearing sessions*
   - *Mentors from the market tech giants*
   - *Cutting-edge Curriculum*

Provides practical experience with 10+ live projects alongside the training
program. Projects challenge students to apply learned skills in real-world
situations. The capstone project, integrated into the final week of the
internship, requires students to apply all learned skills and knowledge.

Hi 23DCS056

Now that you have registered for the Microsoft Developers AI Learning
Hackathon ,
it is time to start thinking about your project!

Here are a few places to get started if you haven't done so already:

1.) Join the Discord Server and
check-in to the hackathon to post technical questions, learn, share, and
support each other.

2.) Looking to form a team? If you want to work in a team to create your
project, navigate over to the participants tab and
search for other participants looking for teammates. You can message them
right from the platform!

3.) Check out the Resources Tab to:

   - Take a look at the technical resources
   - Find inspiration in the example and previous challenge submissions

4.) Check out the special Learning Journey tab to
get the most out of this hackathon!

If you have any hackathon questions, please feel free to reach out via
the Hackathon Discussion Forum!

Happy Building!

Best,
Cassie

To use MATLAB software you need to associate your MathWorks account with a =
license, download the software, install the software, and finally activate =
the software. Please forward this email to additional team members and ask =

ation, tips and tricks, and resources tailored specifically for students. D=
on't forget to let us know how you're using MATLAB & Simulink. Tag us on In=
stagram @matlab_students.

Link to License

If you have not yet created a MathWorks account, you can do so here: https:=
//www.mathworks.com/mwaccount/register

Once you have a MathWorks account, you need to associate it with a license.=
 Your activation key is included in this email and is required to complete =
the association process. Instructions for associating with a license are av=
ailable here: http://www.mathworks.com/matlabcentral/answers/102871

Download and Install

Once you are associated with a license you need to download the software. D=
ownload instructions are available here: http://www.mathworks.com/matlabcen=
tral/answers/98268

The installation will begin as soon as the download is complete.

Activate your Software

Once the software is installed MATLAB will attempt to activate itself. You =
will be required to enter your MathWorks account credentials again for acti=
vation. If the software does not automatically attempt to activate, you wil=
l need to launch the activation client: http://www.mathworks.com/matlabcent=
ral/answers/99457-how-do-i-activate-matlab

In some setups, such as one where a firewall is in place or a proxy is filt=
ering all network activity, you may need to activate MATLAB manually. Instr=
uctions for manual activation can be found here: http://www.mathworks.com/m=
atlabcentral/answers/105854

Attention Required: Posting Queries on GitHub Discussions

Hey,

To streamline our process of addressing queries and to ensure that everyone=
 can benefit from the answers, we kindly request that all queries be posted=
 on our GitHub Discussions page instead of via email.

Please post your questions and concerns in the Q&A category of our GitHub D=
iscussions at the following link: [GitHub Discussions - Q&A](https://7ro79.=
r.sp1-brevo.net/mk/cl/f/sh/7nVU1aA2nfsTSejkWyQjS8qYLOTPzzo/9CIRI44sP8ZQ).

Using GitHub Discussions will help us:

- Solve everyone's queries more efficiently as the GSSoC team will be activ=
ely monitoring the page.
- Keep a track of all queries and responses for future reference.
- Avoid repeated questions, as others will be able to see previously answer=
ed queries.

We appreciate your cooperation and look forward to assisting you on the Git=
Hub platform.

Best regards,
Saksham Shandilya
Community Manager
